<time>1520401584183< /time><Rating>4< /Rating>< Review>
Food is very good and some of the absolute best mexican food in El Dorado County.  Chips and Salsa are both excellent.  Prices are also good for the portions.  The dining area is pretty small but the ambiance is pretty nice. DO NOT GO HERE!!!!!!!!!!!!

I have given my business at least once a month to this place since I was a teenager and have sung it's praises. Well yesterday I ordered what I always order. A meatless item as I have been a vegetarian for the last 15 years of my life. I started eating the Spanish rice and then there was a piece of chicken in my mouth. I spit it out disgusted and looked through the rice and found chicken everywhere inside it. I got really nauseas and threw the whole meal away. I later called to let them know what had happened just to give them a heads up because it's not okay and they should be more careful. The guy on the phone was the tall guy who is always there and he offered me a refund for my meal without me asking for it. He said he would be in the next day and I can come in. So today I walk in and talk to the short guy with the beard and told him there was chicken in my meatless meal yesterday and I was offered a refund. He said, "I'll give you your money back but we will never serve you again." I was obviously perplexed and asked, "what?" He then walked over and said the rice was in front and the chicken was behind it and that there is nothing they can do and I shouldn't complain and should just eat around it it's not a big deal and that they are banning me from the establishment because this is my second complaint. This place and that man whoever he is whether he's just an employee or the owner is EVIL and does not deserve your business ESPECIALLY if you do not eat meat! < Review>
Fantastic deli quality subs with fresh fresh veggies! As far as quality of food, i would give 5 stars. My two gripes with the place is the speed in which the sandwiches are made and the size orientation of the sandwiches. First, all the meat is freshly sliced before its placed on the bread every time. Though it adds to that extra freshness, It can cause a lengthy wait time during busy hours. My biggest problem with the place is they only have 3 sizes. Small (4"), regular (8") and giant (16"). For me, if im hungry and i want a good sized sandwich, an 8 inch sub can leave me a little unsatisfied, but a 16 inch sub is way too much food and pricey. Id like to see them incorporate a large size like 10-12 inches. If none of that bothers you, then its definately a good sandwich chain to try.</Review>

< review>
Mostly we just walk or jog through this park on our daily exercise but its usually full of families large and small and always looks like everyone is having a great time. Lots of dog owners like to play with their animals on the lawn and I have also seen volleyball nets and soccer practice happening on the lawn as well (though its not big enough for a real soccer field.) It's really a fairly small park but big enough for the tiny community it supports I guess. Being right next to a creek full of neat wildlife makes it a great place for a peaceful walk when its quiet enough to hear the birds.< /review>

< review>
Small, intimate environment that's has the vibe of a community pool but it offers so much more.
The slides are exciting and you could see visitors of all shapes and sizes enjoying all four of them. The lazy river is not so lazy but you can easily procure an inflatable and enjoy the movement. The slide entrance is just another plus.
The Wave at the center of the park adds a little bit of excitement that you don't get to experience everywhere. The fun and excitement of boogie boarding on a tsunami in the safe confines of my backyard. Fantastic!
The Olympic sized swimming pool is clean and the abundance of Life Guards makes sure you feel safe at all times.
The kiddie section is a great place for the kids to burn off a little extra energy and have some serious fun!
The park has something for everyone and the prices are so reasonable that it doesn't feel like a burden on the wallet.
Would highly recommend, especially for families!< /review>

<UserId.>106967249746093702194<//UserId.>< user_name>
Alexandra Bourne<//user_name>
< date>
1435357843980< /date>
<rating>4<//rating>< review>
My kids have attended 4 summer camps and they like them. For me as a parent, the summer camps are very affordable and allow the kids to spend some fun time exercising (as opposed to playing video games on the couch). I have been there once for their Duck Race day when they had a $5 entrance special. It was fun, small and I felt that my kids were safe and not wandering off (Since it is small, there is only so many places one can go!). Now, for the bad. Some of the people who go here are not the most "refined" people and kids can be "rough", also, if you leave things unattended they might "disappear". So keep a close eye on your belongings or better yet bring your old stuff so nobody wants to take it. The Snack area also sells their left over food at the end of the day for $1, so that is great for feeding your hungry kids at the end of the day. There is also free parking. Overall, its a great waterpark for locals. Small and very affordable. Also, I recommend signing up for their email newsletter, that is how I heard about the $5 entrance special and got some excellent discounts on summer camps. I also think this is a better park for kids who are good swimmers or a bit older as opposed to very young kids.< /review>

<userid>104301338318969947648<//userid>< Text>
We had a really great afternoon here with our twins (almost 5 years old). Especially because they were allowed to do almost everything (except The Wave itself) which is not the standard in the US. Almost every other place they hardly can get allowed to do anything because they either are to small or to young. Here the life vests are included in admission, which is really good value at $17 for adults and $13 for kids. The staff was very friendly and helpful. The lifeguards were a tad annoying with their exaggerated walking forth and back and swaying their heads in a weird way that didn't seem to serve any purpose, but that's about it. Highly recommendable place for families with kids that can't or won't do high thrilling rides like most of the big water parks have them.</Text>

<name>Amy Paredes<//name><time>1491984872331<//time><rating>3< /rating>< Text>
Dr. Kurian's office is very nice and clean.  His staff is very nice.  Dr. Kurian was very nice and informative and I did not feel rushed through the exam.  While, the hygienist Michelle was very nice and did a great job cleaning my teeth, she went incredibly overboard about telling me how supposedly terrible my gums were, that my gums were bleeding so much "it was like a volcano", that I supposedly had bone loss, and she would classify that I had moderate gingivitis throughout the entire cleaning.  From the moment she walked in and looked at my x-rays to the moment I left.
Dr. Kurian said nothing about this when he examined me and said everything looked good and healthy. Michelle scaring the patient about how terrible their teeth, gums, dental health, etc supposedly are throughout the entire teeth cleaning process is excessive, unnecessary, and unprofessional. I already dislike going to the dentist and having to sit through the scare tactics during the entire cleaning only created more anxiety,  I don't get annoyed easily, but this really annoyed me and really did not make me want to return to this office.  The hygienist also did not do any kind of probing procedure used for actually measuring the pocket depths in the gums to determine levels of gum receding or gingivitis.  Every other dentist I've gone to, has done this procedure, but the hygienist at Dr. Kurian's office did not.  Michelle's conversation throughout my cleaning was loud enough to be heard by the other office employees and therefore loud enough to be heard by anyone else in the office.  It did not provide much in the way of patient privacy and was at the least, very unprofessional and possibly a HIPPAA violation. Whether it were true or not, I certainly wouldn't want all of the rest of the office staff and any other patients in the surrounding areas to know that I was "bleeding like a volcano" or anything else for that matter. Other dentists I've gone to before Dr. Kurian have never said anything like this to me or anything that was cause for concern.  Yet, my first visit here and they're already signing me up for extra cleanings to burn through what my insurance will cover and then have me paying out of pocket for extra services. The appointment and exam was going very well until my experience with Michelle the hygienist.  It is because of that experience that I will most likely not return to Dr. Kurian and will look for another dentist to go to.  This is disappointing because I liked everything else about my experience at Dr. Kurian's office.</Text>

< text>
(Btw this is a long review)I've been volunteering at animal friends connection for about a year now and my family has been fostering dogs for them for a while and they have been wonderful! Most of the complaints are things like they didn't get the animal the wanted, the smell,or the time it took to get the dog. First of all they choose who they think would be best for the dogs. They want them taken care of, to be inside so they aren't neglected, and they don't want an abusive  home. The questioning may seem strict but it was from their heart and love for the animals. You may be mad that you didn't get the animal but they aren't rude they just want a good home. Also its NOT first come first serve they pick who the board thinks would take good care of the animal. They also check your backyard to make sure its fenced in and they aren't going to be put back on the street. If you have a super tiny backyard that no dog can run in and you want a big German Shepard or any other large dog that needs to run, then they most likely aren't going to adopt to you because that poor dog won't be able to exercise. The smell: you can't make a free run animals shelter have no smell of urine or cleaning supplies. Even tho they try to immediately clean up the pee doesn't mean they can watch every dog in there to make sure there's no pee smell.
The ladies hat worj there are super busy making sure all there animals are in the website, getting certain animals and fosters to events, and cleaning up/taking care of Avery animal when there are no volunteers.< /text>

< Text>
While I can genuinely appreciate what this company is doing for animals, they are far from what I would consider a quality adoption or rescue center. My wife and I were in search of a smaller breed, preferably under a year old, and we had seen a few posts online of some potential new furry friends. So we wanted to pay them a visit. First, to even be considered, you have to go through more questions in their application than for the US Military, some absolutely absurd... I understand why, as some new owners dont always make the best pet owners, and conditions can be less than savory... but quite frankly, that's your business, not a rescue centers... if you're looking for a pet, get your stuff together and make sure youre capable of giving them the love and environment they deserve. Back to this place, we arrived without a demanded appointment, and upon entering, the entire place had a smell worse than the dirtiest of county animal shelters. Employees/volunteers sneered up from their phones to give my wife and child a look of disgust when they spat some b.s. opinion of what they think is right and wrong when it came to dogs. Behind the counter, some dogs were stacked in kennels while others were able to mosey around and leave little trails of puddles and piles while employees shrugged it off. Most of the dogs were dirty, some looked malnourished (even after supposedly being there over a month), and the selection was not exactly diverse as far as breeds go. What these people do is use your questionnaire to decide FOR YOU what you get to adopt... but adopt isn't really the right word... it's more like walking into a car dealer knowing what you can afford and want to drive home in, and the car salesman will only sell you the POS because that's his opinion of what you should be driving. Needless to say we found a nice little 2mo old purebred pup online for the same price as shiesty adoption for a dog we "didnt fit", and life is good. If you want a new furry friend from here, brace yourself for the entourage of mind blistering questions that are hyper-invasive on what would normally be a very pleasant experience.< /Text>

< text>
It was a very hot day when the wife and I stopped by to grab a quick something to take home for dinner.  I checked the time, and noted it was 1:PM and we opted to go in side to order hoping it would be a cooler inside.  I ordered a chicken salad and she ordered a standard burger with fries.  My first surprise was Carl's charges $1.00 for the privilege of using my debit card.  Fortunately, I can use the credit card method and they cannot charge me for that.  The order was quickly placed and we sat down to wait for our meal.  I noted it was now 1:05 PM.  We sat and watched as the time went by and eventually we got our food.  At the time of delivery, I looked at my watch again and noted the time was now 1:25PM.  20 minutes to toss a salad and cook up a burger?  When we got home, I sat down to eat the salad and noted it had 3 one inch pieces of chicken sitting on top.  I felt ripped off.  Carl's applies what amounts to a 10 percent tax to your order if you use your debit card, they make you wait 20 minutes for a simple order, and they cheat your order when you finally get it.  I will never do business in this establishment again, nor will I recommend to any of my friends or relatives.<//text>
